There's no way to:\n\t\t//    - Register a service without the authentication middleware\n\t\t//    - Skip authentication for specific methods/services\n\t\t//    - Mark a server as \"internal\" or \"delegated\"\n\n\t\t// Try to create a token, but we can't because we're not authenticated\n\t\t// and there's no way to bypass authentication to create the first token\n\t\ttokenResp, err := client.ListAuthentications(ctx, &authv1.ListAuthenticationsRequest{})\n\n\t\t// This fails, demonstrating the catch-22:\n\t\t// - You need a token to authenticate\n\t\t// - You need to be authenticated to create a token\n\t\t// - There's no way to bootstrap authentication when required=true\n\t\tassert.Error(t, err, \"BUG #2: no mechanism to bypass authentication for internal services\")\n\t\tassert.Nil(t, tokenResp)\n\t\tassert.Equal(t, codes.Unauthenticated, status.Code(err))\n\n\t\t// The root cause: the middleware is applied globally via:\n\t\t// grpc_middleware.WithUnaryServerChain(interceptors...)\n\t\t// where interceptors includes auth_pkg.UnaryInterceptor\n\t\t// There's no way to register a service or method that's exempt from this chain\n\t})\n\n\t// Test 3: Verify that the middleware doesn't have a bypass mechanism\n\tt.Run(\"MiddlewareHasNoBypassMechanism\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\t// The UnaryInterceptor function signature doesn't accept any configuration\n\t\t// to skip certain services or methods. The key issue here is that there's no mechanism to skip authentication. The test should demonstrate that we SHOULD be able to do this, and it fails on the buggy code. Let me think about this more carefully.\n\nActually, the second issue is more about the architecture. The problem is:\n1. Server-Level Authentication Bypass Unavailable (BUG #2)\n**Location**: `/app/cmd/flipt/main.go`\n\nThere is no mechanism to configure certain servers (such as internal/delegated authentication services) to operate without authentication enforcement. All services registered on the gRPC server are equally protected.\n\n**Test Cases**:\n- `UnauthenticatedAuthServiceCallFails`: ✅ PASSES - Correctly rejects unauthenticated calls\n- `NoWayToBypassAuthenticationForSpecificService`: ❌ FAILS - No way to skip auth for internal services\n- `MiddlewareHasNoBypassMechanism`: ✅ PASSES - Documents the architectural limitation\n\n**Root Cause**:\n```go\n// main.go - the middleware is registered globally\nif cfg.Authentication.Required {\n    interceptors = append(interceptors, auth.UnaryInterceptor(logger, authenticationStore))\n}\n\n// All services use the same interceptor chain\ngrpcOpts := []grpc.ServerOption{grpc_middleware.WithUnaryServerChain(interceptors...)}\nsrv := grpc.NewServer(grpcOpts...)\n\n// Register all services on the same server with the same interceptors\npb.RegisterFliptServer(grpcServer, srv)\nauthrpc.RegisterAuthenticationServiceServer(grpcServer, authServer)\nauthrpc.RegisterAuthenticationMethodTokenServiceServer(grpcServer, tokenServer)\n```\n\nThe middleware doesn't have any logic to check:\n- Which service is being called\n- Which method is being called\n- Any configuration to exempt specific services/methods from authentication\n\nThis creates an architectural problem: you need a token to authenticate, but you need to be authenticated to create a token.\n\n## Test Results\n\n### Running the Test\n```bash\ngo test -run TestRegression -v -timeout 60s /workspace/regression_test.go\n```\n\n### Expected Output\nThe test **FAILS** on the
